#  that are capable of editing UTF-8 text files.  The following editors have
#  been confirmed as working properly:
#
#    Visual Studio
#    SciTE
#
#  The following text editors DO NOT WORK, do not use them or you will
#  destroy this file:
#
#    XEmacs
#    EditPlus
